  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ba186cfb-7d15-44c0-b8c7-d09f087a3c61'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer2370154674574487521">Ella and Micha have survived tragedy and heartbreak. When they're together, anything seems possible. But now they are thousands of miles apart, and managing their long distance relationship will put their love to the test.<br/><br/>Ella is back at school, trying hard not worry so much about her future.   <span id="freeText2370154674574487521" style="display:none">Ella and Micha have survived tragedy and heartbreak. When they're together, anything seems possible. But now they are thousands of miles apart, and managing their long distance relationship will put their love to the test.<br /><br />Ella is back at school, trying hard not worry so much about her future. But with her father in and out of rehab, she's having a hard time making it through the days. All she wants is Micha by her side, but she refuses to let her problems get in the way of his dreams.<br /><br />Micha spends his days touring the country with his band, but deep down he knows something is missing. Being away from Ella is harder than he thought it would be. He wants her closer to him-needs her with him. But he won't ask her to leave college, just to be with him.<br /><br />The few moments they do spend together are intense and passionate, but it only makes it more difficult when they have to part. They know they want to be together, but is wanting something enough to get them to their forever?</span>

<div id="review_2482940417" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2482940417" />
    <a title="KAS" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20691061-kas"><img alt="KAS" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1472348331p2/20691061.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2482940417?book_show_action=true">Aug 05, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="KAS" class="user" itemprop="url" name="KAS" href="/user/show/20691061-kas">KAS</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2482940417" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16819556450336478022"><br/><b>Frustratingly Fascinating!!</b><br/><br/>I can tell you nearly every star is for the most patient, forgiving man on the planet, named Micha. Not to mention sexy as all get out and every girl’s dream boyfriend!<br/><br/>I truly grew to love Ella in the novella and the first book of this series, but this girl just gave me pure whiplash and a major headache. I mean ... for crying out loud ... make up your mind already!<br/><br/>Just when Micha and Ella finally seem to get on the same page on where their relationship is heading, Ell</span>
  <span id="freeText16819556450336478022" style="display:none"><br /><b>Frustratingly Fascinating!!</b><br /><br />I can tell you nearly every star is for the most patient, forgiving man on the planet, named Micha. Not to mention sexy as all get out and every girl’s dream boyfriend!<br /><br />I truly grew to love Ella in the novella and the first book of this series, but this girl just gave me pure whiplash and a major headache. I mean ... for crying out loud ... make up your mind already!<br /><br />Just when Micha and Ella finally seem to get on the same page on where their relationship is heading, Ella throws Micha a curve ball, abruptly ending their romance. <br /><br />Let me elaborate ... She ends their dating relationship only wanting to be friends, until the next day she changes her mind, followed by the next day of changing her mind again, and again.<br /><br />Ella is a young woman who is broken and depressed, and is doing her best to “fix” herself. She was never really loved as a child and doesn’t trust herself to love others, nor to love herself. Ella honestly, just wants to be everything Micha deserves.<br /><br />So the back and forth craziness begins. Honestly it is no wonder Micha has a drinking problem!<br /><br />Okay, so maybe his drinking isn’t ALL Ella’s fault. He does have demons of his own he is trying to slay. <br /><br />Thank the stars, Ella totally redeems herself by the end, but still no official HEA. There are two more books to go in this series, so who knows what she’ll do next to drive me batty ;) Guess I will find out shortly.<br /><br />This is a train wreck I am totally addicted to!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />￼</span>
  <a data-text-id="16819556450336478022" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_436691217" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/436691217" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/436691217?book_show_action=true">Oct 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer436691217" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5548223583760387500"><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/7e16d71f-8991-49ac-b511-565ba7981c07_zps8d640979.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394701i/760004._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 7e16d71f-8991-49ac-b511-565ba7981c07_zps8d640979.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Ella and Micha have been through a lot. Both individually and together. Neither one has had an easy life, but they’ve always had each other. After all they have over come, they are finally together. Not just friends, but actually with one another. Things should be great for them, easy, they deserve it. But distance makes things difficult for these two. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/3f14fd73-92fa-4af0-86b2-53559c107b4b_zps25b95773.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394701i/760005._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 3f14fd73-92fa-4af0-86b2-53559c107b4b_zps25b95773.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>Ella is it for me. The way I feel about her is never going to change. I will love her forever.</blockquote>
</b> Micha is touring with his band. He jus</span>
  <span id="freeText5548223583760387500" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/7e16d71f-8991-49ac-b511-565ba7981c07_zps8d640979.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394701i/760004._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7e16d71f-8991-49ac-b511-565ba7981c07_zps8d640979.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Ella and Micha have been through a lot. Both individually and together. Neither one has had an easy life, but they’ve always had each other. After all they have over come, they are finally together. Not just friends, but actually with one another. Things should be great for them, easy, they deserve it. But distance makes things difficult for these two. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/3f14fd73-92fa-4af0-86b2-53559c107b4b_zps25b95773.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394701i/760005._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 3f14fd73-92fa-4af0-86b2-53559c107b4b_zps25b95773.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>Ella is it for me. The way I feel about her is never going to change. I will love her forever.</blockquote>
</b> Micha is touring with his band. He just got a great opportunity, so he is in New York, across the country from his girlfriend Ella. Ella is more than a girlfriend to Micha. She is his best friend, his soulmate. Someone he knows he will spend the rest of his life with. He knows all about Ella’s family problems, guilt etc. and all he wants is to be there for her. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I’ll always be with you, inside and out, through hard times and helpless ones, through love, through doubt.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/c41de5ea-604d-4a06-a0a0-60d8051010f2_zps9e311baf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394701i/760006.jpg" alt=" photo c41de5ea-604d-4a06-a0a0-60d8051010f2_zps9e311baf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>He was the one thing that brought me back out of my dark place. If he leaves me, I’m not sure I can hold on to the light.</blockquote>
</b> Ella is still in Vegas, going to college. She feels the same way about Micha as he does about her. She loves him more than anything, but things with Ella are complicated. The distance is hard on her. Not only that, but her head is a mess. She feels broken. Not good enough for Micha. She isn’t in a good place and she doesn’t want to drag him with her, so she tries to let him go. She really feels like it is best for him. <br><b>
  <blockquote>God, why does my head have to be broken?</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/7f0a66db-9018-4dac-ba37-a23ef24064ae_zps1e6335d1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394701i/760007.jpg" alt=" photo 7f0a66db-9018-4dac-ba37-a23ef24064ae_zps1e6335d1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I understood some of what Ella was going through, and I did sympathize with her. At the same time, it drove me crazy. She just couldn’t stop pushing Micha away. She never wanted to hurt him, but she felt like thats the only way she could get her self together. <br><blockquote>
  <i>People never mean to do things that are hurtful, yet sometimes it just happens, through an intense moment, through brief rationalization, or by simply speaking words that only belong insides on head.<br>Or simply by giving up for a second. <br>People hurt each other all the time.</i>
</blockquote><br>Micha realizes exactly what Ella is doing, and he won’t let her go that eaisly. She can’t be with him, but she is trying to still be his friend and going to therapy to get herself together. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I need to become a person we can both love; otherwise we’ll never make it.</blockquote>
</b><br>Luckily, through all this drama Ella and Micha had their best friends to help them. Did I mention how much I loved Lila and Ethan in this book? YES! They were both fantastic and I am now more excited than ever to get their book! Lila is eventually able to talk some sense into Ella. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Ella, when are you going to realize that you two belong together? Everyone who lays eyes on you can see it and is envious of it because that kind of love isn’t supposed to exist.” <br>“What kind of love are you talking about?”<br> “The kind of love that owns you. The kinds where you know the other person inside and out. Where you can go through hell and back and still make it out okay.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Ella does get herself together. She even gets some closure with her family situation. Ella realizes how much she wants and needs Micha in her life. He is it for her. <br><i>
  <blockquote>I want someone to be mine forever- I want <b>Micha. </b>
</blockquote>
</i> And all I wanted to do was scream... <i>ITS ABOUT DAMN TIME!</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/a5df4a54-bdbf-4bdd-a845-9433771208d7_zps77eb6577.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394701i/760008.jpg" alt=" photo a5df4a54-bdbf-4bdd-a845-9433771208d7_zps77eb6577.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I enjoyed this book. I did. It was frustrating at times, but over all I was happy to get more Ella and Micha... well, mostly more Micha. Micha is the BEST kind of guy. He is sweet, sexy, kind, understanding and just all around perfect for Ella. His life hasn’t been peachy either, but he really tries to make the best of things. Micha will straight up steal your heart! Ella was such a wonderful heroine in the first book. I loved her to pieces... I know she is damaged, she has issues. I get it, I really do. So many times I just wanted to yell at her. Especially when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She lied to Micha and told him she cheated on him... REALLY CHICK? This guy is your best friend and you do him that way? I understand she felt that was the only way she could get him to go, but still- not cool.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I forgive her though, and by the end, I loved her again. I was happy with the conclusion of the story- Jessica Sorensen’s writing is amazing. My wish is that we would have gotten an longer epilogue, or gotten to see a little further into their future. But who knows- maybe in <i>The Temptation of Lila and Ethan</i> we will get a glimpse further into their future ;) Although I didn’t love this one as much as the first, it was still a good read for me!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/62187a3e-206d-477a-aa1b-aa92c476420e_zps8ad2cf91.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394701i/760009.jpg" alt=" photo 62187a3e-206d-477a-aa1b-aa92c476420e_zps8ad2cf91.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5548223583760387500" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer438467463" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8304372983996744481"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760636._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>MICHA SCOTT</b> Look at those eyes, that lip ring...Oh Micha ❤❤❤❤singer, song-writer, guitar player .... Swoon ❤<br/><br/>I don't even want to <b>explain</b> how it hurts my book heart to not give this book 5 stars. Although, Ella in most parts of this book was an <b>EPIC FAIL</b> to me......Micha ❤definitely delivered. It cut me <b>deep</b> to see less than magnanimous reviews of this book about their <b>FOREVER<b> as I loved "The Secret of Ella and Micha" with all my heart. Seriously all of it. Micha ❤has been my reining book boyfrie</b></b></span>
  <span id="freeText8304372983996744481" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760636._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>MICHA SCOTT</b> Look at those eyes, that lip ring...Oh Micha ❤❤❤❤singer, song-writer, guitar player .... Swoon ❤<br><br>I don't even want to <b>explain</b> how it hurts my book heart to not give this book 5 stars. Although, Ella in most parts of this book was an <b>EPIC FAIL</b> to me......Micha ❤definitely delivered. It cut me <b>deep</b> to see less than magnanimous reviews of this book about their <b>FOREVER<b> as I loved "The Secret of Ella and Micha" with all my heart. Seriously all of it. Micha ❤has been my reining book boyfriend for the longest time.....since like November 2012. You know since I'm fickle. This is HUGE!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760637.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>MICHA</b> ❤His level of GREATNESS can not even be expressed. He was perfect. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760638._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760639._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>His weakness :<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760640._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>ELLA DANIELS</b><br><br>and boy did she bring him low..on a repetitive daily basis..It made me want to <br><br><b>cut-a-bitch</b><br><br>..She loved breaking his heart into little pieces.....taking mine with it..... <br><br>So the story opens up with Ella having these recurrent dreams:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760641._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Every night I have the same dream. Micha and I are standing on opposite ends of the bridge. Micha extends his hand and I walk toward him, but he slips away from me until he lands up on the railing of the bridge. He teeters in the wind and I want to save him, but my feet won't budge. A gust of wind slams into him and he falls backward, vanishing into the darkness. I wake up screaming full of guilt</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760642.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760643.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>It feels like we're slipping away from each other, and he was the one thing that brought me back out of my dark place. If he leaves me, I'm not sure I can hold onto the light</i><br><br>Micha is touring with his band and it leads him to New York. Ella is in Vegas. I get it people, distance <b>sucks</b> but COME ON.....you've been each others rock since you were children. A little distance....Its a bridge you can handle. This is the beginning of when things went all wrong for me with Ella. I totally wanted to understand where she was coming from...depression, guilt, fear...but some decisions she made...I was not a fan! She broke the cardinal rule !!! No recovery !!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760644.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>uggggggggg WHY ? Why would you just obliterate a genuine heart ? And then go from this intense love....to ...."let's just be friends"...<br><br><b>WTF?????</b> NO NO NO NO NO NO<br><br><i>I'm letting him go. Cutting the strings. Because I love him that much</i><br><br><i>I need to become a person we both can love; otherwise we'll never make it</i><br><br><i>I want him to hate me, just as mush as I hate myself. That way I can't bring him down with me</i><br><br>SCREAM !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! she <b>SLICED OPEN</b> Micha's heart!!!!<br><br>See because Micah believes in this...LOVE....<br><b>THE KIND OF LOVE THAT OWNS YOU. THE KIND WHERE YOU KNOW THE OTHER PERSON INSIDE AND OUT. WHERE YOU CAN GO THROUGH HELL AND BACK AND STILL MAKE IT OUT OK</b><br><br><i>Ella is it for me. The way I feel about her is never going to change. I will love her forever, but I need her closer to me, not thousands of miles away. How am I supposed to tell her, though, that I'm ready to begin her future, when I know she has no clue what her future is yet?</i><br><br>OH MY GOD...my book heart was not happy...I had so many things Ella said highlighted but then when i re-read....<br><br>still induced the same....eye-rolling and wanting to <b>vomit blood</b>....<br><br>I cant even go into how much redemption she needed to make good with me!!! I tried to be compassionate because of the situation but....time after time....I just screamed <br><br><b>GET YOUR SHIT TOGETHER PRETTY GIRL</b> <br><br>ok my rant is done. I am no longer going to rehash bad memories. I am going to end this with some big Micha ❤love because that is what he deserves....Mental images...to eradicate the nerve-triggering moments<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760645._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760646.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760647.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760648.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><span>[image error]</span><br>finally never too late for some Ella redemption....she put that RING on .....<br><br>Wow I needed those pictures....I needed to leave this page with a case of the <b>FEEL GOODS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760650._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Micha's still got it......he was all-around perfect. Luckily....he got his Forever<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394963i/760651.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>4 Forever and ever and ever, but I needed 5 magnanimous Micha Stars !!!</b></b></b></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/472135579?book_show_action=true">Dec 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty">Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer472135579" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11863639522293940784"><br/><br/> <br/> <br/><b>“You left me, ripped out my heart, and then came back acting like a robot, and you know what? We made it through. You and I, good or bad, belong together. We make each other whole.”</b><br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774778.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I love the way this book is written in alternate POV’s. The only reason why I couldn’t give this 5 stars was because of the Ending. I needed more.. it felt rushed and unfinished somehow…<br/> <br/>This Book picks up from The Secret of Ella and Micha, where Ella is back at school and Micha is touring the country with his band</span>
  <span id="freeText11863639522293940784" style="display:none"><br><br> <br> <br><b>“You left me, ripped out my heart, and then came back acting like a robot, and you know what? We made it through. You and I, good or bad, belong together. We make each other whole.”</b><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774778.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love the way this book is written in alternate POV’s. The only reason why I couldn’t give this 5 stars was because of the Ending. I needed more.. it felt rushed and unfinished somehow…<br> <br>This Book picks up from The Secret of Ella and Micha, where Ella is back at school and Micha is touring the country with his band.<br>They are thousands of miles apart and miss each other terribly and they are both miserable without each other.<br> <br>Ella wont tell Micha to give up his dream and nor will Micha tell Ella to leave school. When they find ways to meet each other everything is perfect.<br><br>Micha...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774779._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Ella is it for me. The way I feel about her is never going to change. I will love her forever, but I need her closer to me, not thousands of miles away."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774780.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ella...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774781._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their chemistry is electrifying!<br> <br><b> “When his lips return to mine, it's not just about lust or desire - it's about making us whole.”</b><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774782.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But all good things must come to an end… and Ella must go back to school and Micha will continue his touring.<br><br><b>"It isn’t as important to feel great about all the things we do,” I say softly. “But how we feel toward the end when we look back at everything we’ve done.”</b><br> <br>When Ella gets a call to say her father is out of rehab, she goes into panic! Only this time she doesn’t want to call Micha to help her because she needs to do these things on her own--- finding a way home to go back to her drunken father.<br><br><b>"I hate to say this Ella, but your father is fucking weak. He can’t blame what he does on anyone but himself. And I’m not him and you’re not your mom. Just because their story ended badly doesn’t mean our will.”"</b><br> <br>Ella is struggling within herself with her ghosts of her past, what happened that night…<br>She feels alone… and the only one she wants by her side is Micha.<br>Again she refuses to call him with her problems and drag him down so she feels like she needs to set him fre<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774783.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Free of her problems and her messed up head.<br>She needs Micha to be happy. She loves him that much to let him go..<br><br><b>"I’m letting him go. Cutting the strings. Because I love him that much."</b><br><br>So she lies to Micha and breaks his heart and breaks hers too in the process…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774784._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b> “Ella, when are you going to realize that you two belong together? Everyone who lays eyes on you can see it and is envious of it because that kind of love isn't supposed to exist."<br><br>"What kind of love are you talking about?"<br><br>"The kind of love that owns you. The kind where you know the other person inside and out. Where you can go through hell and back and still make it out ok.”</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380743583i/3118215.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Ella goes through a deep depression, has an emotional breakdown and suffers a lot with her mental issues. She sees a therapist through it all and every answer to anything leads to Micha…<br>Her Rock..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400053ra/774785.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Micha is so heart broken, he cannot believe what Ella told him and still then he loves her…<br><br><b>"When she’s ready, she’ll tell… at least I hope. But what if she doesn’t? What if I’ve spent my life chasing a ghost?"</b><br> <br>We get glimpses into the past of Ella and Micha as kids and even before they got together they probably loved each other.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774786._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b> “That's because you loved me. You just didn't know it yet." <br><br>"You didn't know it either. You were just as blind as me.”</b><br> <br>The rest of the book we see Micha and Ella working through their problems… Both of them have problems with their pasts and families.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774787.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>There is a lot of back and forth with Ella and it is frustrating at times because we know how deep the love she has for Micha is.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774788.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I’m sorry, pretty girl, but you really don’t get to choose what I want, what I do, or who I get to be with. So unless you want me to leave you because you don’t love me anymore, I’m not going anywhere."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774789.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>It got a bit irritating that Ella is running and Micha is the one running after her most of the time.<br><br><b>"I love him so much there are no words to describe it. I’m extremely lucky to have him. I make a promise to myself that I will work on giving him what he wants and try to make him happy."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774790.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But that’s just how Micha is… and how he feels… these two have such a deep bond and connection and can read each others mind like no other.<br><br><b>"For the rest of my life?” His voice softens. “Do you want that, Ella May? Do you want me eternally, infinitely, forever, till death do us part?”"</b><br><br><b>"It will, and you want to know why?” I ask and she nods. “Because most people go into this blind. They don’t know the bad side of the person they’re with. But we know each other’s flaws and cracks—we know what we’re getting into and that makes us stronger"<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774791.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>"Like how I know that right now you want to leave. Not because you don’t love me, but because you’re scared. Scared you can’t do it. Scared you’ll hurt me. Scared you’ll actually be happy about what I’m going to ask you.”<br></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774792.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>This is an unforgettable love story filled with many emotions… acceptance… recovery…hope… and <b>FOREVER</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400053i/774793.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="11863639522293940784" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_763254514" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/763254514" />
    <a title="Sandra " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9752625-sandra"><img alt="Sandra " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345749155p2/9752625.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/763254514?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sandra " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandra " href="/user/show/9752625-sandra">Sandra </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=omfg">omfg</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=sexy-males">sexy-males</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=sad">sad</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=reviewed-books">reviewed-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=continuing-series">continuing-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer763254514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12181390071098716009"><b>ROUNDING UP TO 2.5 STARS.</b><br/><br/><i>The Forever of Ella and Micha</i> is the 2nd book in <i>The Secret</i> trilogy, and to be honest i'm a little disappointed with it since i thought the first book was really good, and this one didn't exactly reach my expectations. So yeah, i was let down. <br/><br/><a target='_blank' title='ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting' href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/593/yb9.gif/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384698534ra/6934459.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://imageshack.us' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><a target='_blank' title='ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting' href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/43/uxe8.jpg/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384697157i/6934249.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://imageshack.us' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/>When Ella and Micha are together everything seems possible, but now they are miles apart. <br/><br/>Ella has be through a lot and is still trying to overcome her past for a chance of a better future. <b>Will she succeed?</b><br/><br/><a target='_blank' title='ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting' href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/191/cnbe.jpg/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384700418i/6934710.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://imageshack.us' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/>Micha is bus</span>
  <span id="freeText12181390071098716009" style="display:none"><b>ROUNDING UP TO 2.5 STARS.</b><br><br><i>The Forever of Ella and Micha</i> is the 2nd book in <i>The Secret</i> trilogy, and to be honest i'm a little disappointed with it since i thought the first book was really good, and this one didn't exactly reach my expectations. So yeah, i was let down. <br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/593/yb9.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384698534ra/6934459.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/43/uxe8.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384697157i/6934249.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>When Ella and Micha are together everything seems possible, but now they are miles apart. <br><br>Ella has be through a lot and is still trying to overcome her past for a chance of a better future. <b>Will she succeed?</b><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/191/cnbe.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384700418i/6934710.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>Micha is busy touring the country with his band, but instead of fully enjoying himself doing what he loves, missing Ella is tearing him apart. He wants her with him, but will not ask her to leave collage and everyone behind for him. <br> <br><b>Sacrifices have to be made to get them the 'forever' they want.... but is there such thing as an everlasting love? <br><br>"What kind of love are you talking about?" <br>"The kind of love that owns you. The kind where you know the other person inside and out. Where you can go through hell and back and still make it out ok.”</b> <br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/844/v2oo.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384698534ra/6934460.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><b>Let me start from <u>Micha</u>.</b> <br><b>About 20% through the book i'm thinking</b> "Who the FUCK are you, and what have you done to my Micha?" <br>I did not even recognize him and thought he changed quite a lot. <br><b>I swear all he nearly thought about was sex</b>, and to be honest that's really all that happened between him and Ella. I liked that there was more 'action' between them, but seriously, after a while it gets annoying. <b>We get enough guys that think and act like Micha in the real world, thank you very much.</b> <br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/209/80.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384701746ra/6934851.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><b>
  <u>Ella </u>
</b><br>...ermm... lets just say <b>at times i really did think she was a little bit crazy</b> (you know, just a tiny bit *cough*). And omg, i HATED with all my heart the therapy sessions she went to. <br>NOT a big fan of therapists, just reading about them makes me want to punch the wall and destroy everything. <br><b>At times i did indeed like Ella. <br>I think she is the kind of protagonist most readers have a love/hate relationship with</b><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/10/lxq.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384701746ra/6934852.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><b>The ending was cute and i liked it.</b> <br>It was heartwarming to see how Ella and her family slowly fix their relationship. But i admit i kind of <b>hate her brother</b> - what an asshole. <br><br>Having the paperback version i was lucky enough to get a sneak peek of <b>Lila and Ethan's story, which I AM SO EXCITED ABOUT</b>! It's going to be amazing, i can tell ;)<br><br>Overall, this was a <b>nice love story about moving on</b>, <b>forgiving</b>, and perhaps <b>second chances</b>. The 3rd book (<i>The Ever After of Ella and Micha</i>) is coming out 3rd Dec 2013, and i'm definitely in for the ride!<br><br><br><br> <b></b><br><i></i><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_437696382" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/437696382" />
    <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance"><img alt="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481665315p2/10247668.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/437696382?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance">Katy Loves Romance ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17560336-the-forever-of-ella-and-micha">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=top-favourite-reads-of-all-time">top-favourite-reads-of-all-time</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer437696382" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4638753797185154648"> <b>3.5 Micha Stars!!!</b><br/><br/>I absolutely loved and adored <i>The secret of Ella and Micha</i>, it left me with a real book hangover and I've been counting down the months for it to come out I was like......<br/><br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/laughinggif_zps61257f48.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394851ra/760380.gif' alt=' photo laughinggif_zps61257f48.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>However I didn't enjoy it as much as I had hoped!! <br/><br/>We begin there story pretty much where we left from, Ella is struggling her guilt with her past and all that she has to deal with her father. <br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/The%20forever%20ella%20and%20micha/foreverellaandmicha_zps7b6bc7fb.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394851i/760381.jpg' alt=' photo foreverellaandmicha_zps7b6bc7fb.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Ella and Micha have been best friends since they were kids, they know each other inside and out, and they mak</span>
  <span id="freeText4638753797185154648" style="display:none"> <b>3.5 Micha Stars!!!</b><br><br>I absolutely loved and adored <i>The secret of Ella and Micha</i>, it left me with a real book hangover and I've been counting down the months for it to come out I was like......<br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/laughinggif_zps61257f48.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394851ra/760380.gif" alt=" photo laughinggif_zps61257f48.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>However I didn't enjoy it as much as I had hoped!! <br><br>We begin there story pretty much where we left from, Ella is struggling her guilt with her past and all that she has to deal with her father. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/The%20forever%20ella%20and%20micha/foreverellaandmicha_zps7b6bc7fb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394851i/760381.jpg" alt=" photo foreverellaandmicha_zps7b6bc7fb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Ella and Micha have been best friends since they were kids, they know each other inside and out, and they make each other whole. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/The%20forever%20ella%20and%20micha/kidsellaandmicha_zps3ca149cf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394851i/760382.jpg" alt=" photo kidsellaandmicha_zps3ca149cf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"The kind where you know the other person inside and out. Where you can go through hell and back and still make it out okay."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Ella goes back to study in Vegas and Micha is on the road with his band, they struggle with there separation and Ella is struggling with her past/depression/anxiety, she's seeing a counsellor which is helping but there's a whole lot of ups and downs in this one!! <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/The%20forever%20ella%20and%20micha/Ella-and-Micah_zps3b60445f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394851i/760383.jpg" alt=" photo Ella-and-Micah_zps3b60445f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Whenever they get together though, I still felt their love shine through and I also still felt connected to them as a couple..<br><br>There is a fair amount of steam.<br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/The%20forever%20ella%20and%20micha/kisingincar_zps735baa74.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394851ra/760384.gif" alt=" photo kisingincar_zps735baa74.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and also a lot of hardship and upset.<br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/The%20forever%20ella%20and%20micha/hugginggif_zps65db869a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394851ra/760385.gif" alt=" photo hugginggif_zps65db869a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And a good amount of romance.<br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/The%20forever%20ella%20and%20micha/ellaandmicha2_zps171e431c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394851i/760386.jpg" alt=" photo ellaandmicha2_zps171e431c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Ok so let's get to the review!! as I say when I read the secret of Ella and Micha I stayed awake all night, I couldn't put it down, I didn't get frustrated and I loved it from start to finish. I still enjoyed this one I just didn't love it, Why? because I really didn't expect this story to go down the path it went on, the book is called <b>the forever Ella and Micha</b> so I expected a lot of happy times and when you finished the last book I thought it ended pretty well, In this story there's a whole lot of Ella pushing Micha away and there is a lot of back and forth, I do understand at times why Ella felt the way she did but I also know when you got something good stick with it and lean on it!! Micha in my mind was AWESOME, he was what Ella needed him to be at every step of the way and very very <b>patient</b>.<br><br>I did love them, they do have a strong connection, throughout the book I still Adored Micha he made it for me, pulled them through it, helped Ella see what they have and why they should fight and stay together and be strong. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Love you more than life itself, more than the sun and the air. You own my soul, Ella May. Micha</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Micha was definitely the strength, kept loving Ella at every obstacle and every turn he stole my heart 100% throughout the whole book. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"You and I, good and bad, belong together. We make each other whole."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I loved Ethan and Lila as well, so comical kept the spirit up and kept nudging them in the right direction.Really great friends and some real fun times drinking, singing, car racing etc. So I will keep reading this series because I love Jessica's writing it flows nicely, she's easy to understand, she's passionate about the characters in the story but I just wanted more!!<br><br>I would of bumped the star to up if the epilogue was longer as I felt like it ended abruptly, therefore I really hope in Ethan and Lila's story we see a happy Ella and Micha and a complete story leaving me feeling like I did at the end of the secret of Ella and Micha. There is a HEA at the end but In my mind it isn't <b>COMPLETE</b>!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/The%20forever%20ella%20and%20micha/66bc9cfa-69d3-4643-a025-2165a8b6e9a8_zps73d0243c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394851i/760387._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 66bc9cfa-69d3-4643-a025-2165a8b6e9a8_zps73d0243c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/The%20forever%20ella%20and%20micha/a9956246-86dd-411d-aa34-ffcbd09bbdf7_zps4f7f8711.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394851i/760388._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo a9956246-86dd-411d-aa34-ffcbd09bbdf7_zps4f7f8711.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So if your wanting an Intense love story, that's also passionate and pretty fast pasted even if it's just for Micha go read, I would recommend this story to anyone who enjoyed thoughless and effortless!!! which I also adored by the way.....<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Micha, I love you, "I murmur between breaths and relize that this is what I want. Forever.</b>
</blockquote><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4638753797185154648" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="*.Amaia.* BlackMagicRose" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose"><img alt="*.Amaia.* BlackMagicRose" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435489639p2/14475340.jpg" /></a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17560336-the-forever-of-ella-and-micha">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose?shelf=rock-star">rock-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose?shelf=youngadult-newadult">youngadult-newadult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose?shelf=abuse-mental-disorder-neglect">abuse-mental-disorder-neglect</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer626599085" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2242736921188755305"><b>3 1/5 STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423216i/843071._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>Ella and Micha's story</b> continues in this second book of the series. Best friends since their childhood and now lovers, they will both have to face the problems that having a romantic relationship brings. <b>Distance is going to be one of their first enemies</b> when they both try to make their love story work and at the same time fulfill their dreams. <b>The future and the past</b> are hunting Ella and Micha, and they have to decide which one are willing to let go. Trust issues. jelousy, lack of h</span>
  <span id="freeText2242736921188755305" style="display:none"><b>3 1/5 STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423216i/843071._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Ella and Micha's story</b> continues in this second book of the series. Best friends since their childhood and now lovers, they will both have to face the problems that having a romantic relationship brings. <b>Distance is going to be one of their first enemies</b> when they both try to make their love story work and at the same time fulfill their dreams. <b>The future and the past</b> are hunting Ella and Micha, and they have to decide which one are willing to let go. Trust issues. jelousy, lack of honesty, fear and the shadow of their past will make them <b>doubt if they are really meant to be together, forever.</b> <br><br>I really didn't know what to expect from this book. I enjoyed the first one, but didn't love it, for some reason <b>I never got close to either Ella or Micha</b>. I wanted to try and give these two a chance in this second book, and even if I enjoyed it and I really got closer to them, it wasn't enough. But I got to read some <b>really sweet moments</b> and that's the reason I finally gave this book 4 stars instead of 3 (actually 3 1/5).<br><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Best parts of the story:</u>
</b><br><br><b>- Ella and Micha's Friendship:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423216i/843072.jpg" width="400" height="267'" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>- Micha:</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423216i/843073._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600'" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <u>Worst part of the story:</u>
</b><br><br><b>- The constant break-up/make-up:</b><br><br>I get that both Ella and Micha have a lot of baggage, but some of their fights were ridiculous and they really pissed me off. But well, I guess you sometimes hurt the person you love the most.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423216i/843074._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600'" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>

<div id="review_571422634" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/571422634?book_show_action=true">Mar 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=the-bad-boy-look">the-bad-boy-look</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer571422634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer487298819632739633"><b>Rating Clarification: 3.5 Stars</b>	<br/><br/>In this second book Ella and Micha are trying to get past their problems while trying to make a long-distance-relationship work. <br/>Micha is having some family issues, he always on the road with the band, misses Ella like crazy and somehow alcohol seems a pretty good way to deal with the problems. <br/>Ella is taking the distance pretty bad and her depressions is worst again, so she’s slowing falling again to the dark place that made her run the first time.<br/>So they find th</span>
  <span id="freeText487298819632739633" style="display:none"><b>Rating Clarification: 3.5 Stars</b>	<br><br>In this second book Ella and Micha are trying to get past their problems while trying to make a long-distance-relationship work. <br>Micha is having some family issues, he always on the road with the band, misses Ella like crazy and somehow alcohol seems a pretty good way to deal with the problems. <br>Ella is taking the distance pretty bad and her depressions is worst again, so she’s slowing falling again to the dark place that made her run the first time.<br>So they find that forever is a really hard thing to achieve and sometimes things are more complicated that they seem in the beginning. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380366186ra/718408.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really liked the first book. For real. The premise was great, the main characters were great together, the supporting characters were pretty good. <br>All of that was again in this book, including the great premise, but somehow was just <i>meh</i>.<br>Now I feel like I've waited months for nothing, I'm kind of disappointed. <br>I spent most of the book wanting to pull my own hair and doing something like this: <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380365814ra/717965.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I got a little annoyed with Micha, but Ella took the prize home. Really, she have a great boyfriend, who would do anything for her and knows all her problems and STILL loves her… and all she do is basically wonder if she is going mental one day. <br>THIS HAPPENS THROUGH THE WHOLE BOOK.<br><i> Ella thinks she’s crazy and Micha is too good for her - Ella makes something to send him away - he chases her anyway – he does something stupid</i><br>No, really, the WHOLE book. It’s frustrating. Most of the book I just wanted to slap some sense into them. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414904ra/818532.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But even with all the craziness and frustration, I liked the book and was nice to see the ending to their story. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The ring thing was really sweet. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The epilogue was pretty good... but it should have been way longer.<br>If you liked the first one, you really should read this. ;) <br>(But don’t fool yourselves, the first was way better!) </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_524899673" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/524899673" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/524899673?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone, especially Katie McGarry fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=review-requests">review-requests</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers">keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=covers-to-covet">covers-to-covet</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer524899673" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5610443440227214613"><a href='http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2013/05/arc-review-the-forever-of-ella-and-micha-by-jessica-sorensen.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333934i/693541.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This book….*sigh* I think I have been rendered speechless. I’ve read quite a lot of books, but I don’t think I’ve ever felt an emotional connection to characters as much as I have with Ella and Micha. If you loved book one, THE FOREVER OF ELLA AND MICHA will blow you away. It’s more angsty, darker, sexier, bigger and better! Sorensen gives it her all and it’s such a magical thing!<br/><br/>Ella and Micha have been through a lot already, both individually and as a couple. Their love has been tested and</span>
  <span id="freeText5610443440227214613" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2013/05/arc-review-the-forever-of-ella-and-micha-by-jessica-sorensen.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333934i/693541.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book….*sigh* I think I have been rendered speechless. I’ve read quite a lot of books, but I don’t think I’ve ever felt an emotional connection to characters as much as I have with Ella and Micha. If you loved book one, THE FOREVER OF ELLA AND MICHA will blow you away. It’s more angsty, darker, sexier, bigger and better! Sorensen gives it her all and it’s such a magical thing!<br><br>Ella and Micha have been through a lot already, both individually and as a couple. Their love has been tested and tried before, but when Micha goes on tour with his band, they are separated for months at a time and that takes a serious strain on their relationship.<br><br>Ella continues to have her problems and to be honest, they feel more prominent and all-consuming in this serving. Sorensen definitely doesn’t shy away from the darkness. She meets it front and center and for Ella, it’s a damn scary thing. As a reader, it pulls on your heartstrings to witness this, but also I love the way that Ella has manned up to her problems. She calls herself “a brat with mental problems” and though she jokes about it, her even saying that shows that she is already coming to understand herself on a different level. She is healing and she is looking for help. Her therapist, Anna was interesting to me because I studied Psychology in university and it just fit all my interests. I wanted to see Ella get better and I am thrilled to see her happy. As I said, I felt a kinship with her character and have come to love her despite her flaws.<br><br>Micha…oh Micha. Could a guy be more perfect? In the last book, Sorensen lays the foundation to Micha’s problems but she doesn’t really explore it. In this book, we get it in full throttle. Micha has a dark side and though not too damaging, you still feel for him. His relationship with his father is so flawed that it begins to take a toll on him. Resentment builds and when Micha’s father asks for a favor that seems too much, Micha doesn’t know how to handle it.<br><br>Lila and Ethan also have their own problems and although they aren’t explored fully in this book, you get a sense of them. I cannot wait to read THE TEMPTATION OF LILA AND ETHAN to hear more about their problems. I sense it has to do with their parents. And also, how about Ethan’s answer to the “What are you thankful for?” question? Red lacy bras? And what about Lila’s answer? Candy canes? I NEED TO KNOW! You can be sure I will get this book the second it comes out. I’ve become so invested into these characters, it’s almost a scary thing. <br><br>I also have to mention the smexy times in this book because even though that shower scene in book one was smokin’ hot. FOREVER has soo many amazing sex scenes, I couldn’t keep track of which one was my favorite. The car scene and possibly the poker scene were amongst my top faves though. Oh wait! And the wedding scene too. Basically any scene where Micha talks dirty is my favorite.<br><br>THE FOREVER OF ELLA AND MICHA feels like a true NA book. It’s more reckless than the first, more darker, more intense and more heartbreaking, but every second is worth the ride. Like first true love, I fell in love alongside Ella and Micha again, remembering the intense emotions of figuring out what you want and who you want to be.<br><br>On the surface, THE FOREVER OF ELLA AND MICHA is a fun, sexy, unforgettable story of first love. But at its core, it’s also an emotional story about acceptance, recovery and hope.<br><br>Sorensen is hands down my favorite New Adult author. Blending the sweet, the reckless, and the heartbreaking together into an enticing mix, her books will drown you until all you can think about are her characters. Clear your keeper shelf, because this book deserves its own covet spot!<br><br>*ARC provided by publisher<br><br>Favorite Quote:<br>“I’ll always be with you, inside and out. Through hard times and helpless ones, through love, through doubt.”<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5610443440227214613" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_432483199" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/432483199" />
    <a title="Sara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10747133-sara"><img alt="Sara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1468189168p2/10747133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/432483199?book_show_action=true">Oct 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara" href="/user/show/10747133-sara">Sara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10747133-sara?shelf=books-in-a-series">books-in-a-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer432483199" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5017683119778549888">The would have been a 5 star read for me if it wasn't for the ending. I love Micha and Ella. LOVE. Ella is not an annoying heroin. She's the most giving one. Ella has always had the brunt of her families issues to carry. She was responsible for watching over her mom. Making sure she took her meds. When her mom died, she was blamed. At 17 years old. How wrong is that? Her dad and her brother made her feel like it was her fault. Then she was responsible for her drunk dad, paying the bills, keeping</span>
  <span id="freeText5017683119778549888" style="display:none">The would have been a 5 star read for me if it wasn't for the ending. I love Micha and Ella. LOVE. Ella is not an annoying heroin. She's the most giving one. Ella has always had the brunt of her families issues to carry. She was responsible for watching over her mom. Making sure she took her meds. When her mom died, she was blamed. At 17 years old. How wrong is that? Her dad and her brother made her feel like it was her fault. Then she was responsible for her drunk dad, paying the bills, keeping house, cooking and whatever else came her way. Dean took off as soon as he could because he's a selfish prick. She's never had anyone take care of her. Except Micha. To me Micha is the only person who ever considered her feelings. He genuinely cared for her and her happiness. And he was also undeniably in love with her. Ella tried to push him away. To her, he would be better off without her and her issues. She convinced herself she was sick like her mom. Micha wanted to be a musician, but at what cost? These two grew up in this book. Or should I say they finally saw the bigger picture. Ethan gave some great advice. Lila was a terrific friend. I loved those two. Ella's therapist really got this girl to see her and her life growing up for what it was. And taught her to heal and move on. Dean is still a first class prick, right alongside Micha's dad. Ella's dad finally stepped into his parental shoes, after much anguish and sobriety. The only thing I didn't like so much was the ending. I felt like there was a good flow to the book until about 90%. Then it was over and the epilogue was only 6 months into the future and it didn't give me any real insight to their lives moving forward. After reading this is spent about an hour pissed off. I just needed more. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5017683119778549888" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText4210160948620323788" style="display:none">The Secret of Ella and Micha is where this story all started. Ella went off to college and comes home looking completely different. Gone is the wild child and in her place is a girl Micha doesn't recognize. She is preppy and she is a rule follower. The Ellie Mae Micha knows is rebel, a fighter and a racer.<br><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396550i/764416._SX540_.jpg" width="346" height="230" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Micha Scott is not the same boy he was before either. He is going after what he has always known he wanted, and that is Ella. Micha is in for the long haul. His career is taking off and Micha is on the road with his band. The strain of separation is difficult but they have a deeper relationship than most. They have a shared history that goes back for what seems like... forever.<br><br><em>"Snorting a laugh, I press my palm to his and I swear the earth stops, because this moment is the beginning of forever."</em> -Ella<br><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396550i/764417.jpg" width="402" height="402" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ella is struggling with her family, her past and the guilt that eats away at her every day about her mother's suicide. But neither knows if it will be enough.<br><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396550i/764418.jpg" width="287" height="202" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They both fall back on old habits and when things get tough, they try and escape. I absolutely <strong>LOVE</strong> all of their broken pieces. I <strong>LOVE</strong> that together they are stronger than they are apart. I <strong>LOVE</strong> that they know every detail about one another and can read each other like an open book. I <strong>LOVE</strong> Ella's journey and the revelations that happen. I <strong>LOVE</strong> that Micha doesn't compromise and he doesn't give in. I <strong>LOVE</strong> this book!<br><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396550ra/764420.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“Micha, I love you,” I murmur between breaths and realize that this is what I want. Forever.</i>- Ella<br><br>This book left me with a warm fuzzy feeling. I was really afraid to read this because there were a few reviews that were not complimentary. I loved the first one so much! This one was just as good in my ever so humble opinion. I really want there to be another one...does that make me a bad person...I don't think so.<br><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396550ra/764421.gif" width="246" height="160" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>5 HUGE Soul Mate Stars<br></span>
