<span id="freeTextContainer10105742436647792165">I was SO excited for this sequel... And then... <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406669ra/793728.gif' width='500' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374503ra/728592.gif' width='500' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15717876.The_Secret_of_Ella_and_Micha__The_Secret___1_' title='The Secret of Ella and Micha (The Secret, #1) by Jessica Sorensen' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Secret of Ella and Micha</a> was angst-ridden, highly emotional, and red-HOT-spicy. The sequel... <i>not so much</i>. Yeah, there was an abundance of "sexy" scenes littered throughout the book - no complaints there - BUT, it just lacked <i>substance.</i> (pleasedontshootme?)<br/><br/>Not to mention... Ella and Micha's issues this time around, started getting BEYOND repetitive; I found myself skimming through A LOT. And, I usually NEVER just skim through stuff. So yeah. No</span>
  <span id="freeText10105742436647792165" style="display:none">I was SO excited for this sequel... And then... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406669ra/793728.gif" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374503ra/728592.gif" width="500" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15717876.The_Secret_of_Ella_and_Micha__The_Secret___1_" title="The Secret of Ella and Micha (The Secret, #1) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Secret of Ella and Micha</a> was angst-ridden, highly emotional, and red-HOT-spicy. The sequel... <i>not so much</i>. Yeah, there was an abundance of "sexy" scenes littered throughout the book - no complaints there - BUT, it just lacked <i>substance.</i> (pleasedontshootme?)<br><br>Not to mention... Ella and Micha's issues this time around, started getting BEYOND repetitive; I found myself skimming through A LOT. And, I usually NEVER just skim through stuff. So yeah. Not good. <br><br>In short (not in any particular order): <br>1. I was bored. And annoyed.<br>2. Issues were repetitive<br>3. STUPID HEROINE ALERT<br>4. Mediocre (at best) execution, and ending. (Totally predictable, cheese-ball ending.) <br>5. Sex scenes were lacking *oomph* &amp; that little something called: CHEMISTRY. <br>6. All around flat characters<br>7. Boring plot<br><br>But honestly, I lost interest after <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ella tells Micha the ridiculous lie about her cheating on him, in order to get him to break up with her. WHY? Because she felt "undeserving" of his love... (puke). Then, Micha goes into a "dirty dog" sex-crazed frenzy, banging random women left &amp; right. *pulls hair out* ...Like, what's new? Other than the whole scenario being unnecessary and GROSS. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>OK, so let me elaborate a bit further on my #3 and #6. Basically, the emotional, broken, yet vulnerable, and extremely complex Ella from the first book just disappeared. This time around, her character just fell completely FLAT. <br><br>Suddenly, she transformed into the most pitiful, self-deprecating "non-heroine" ever. She frustrated the living daylights out of me. I wanted to hide. On the same note, MICHA acted totally out-of-character, or maybe played into the whole "bad boy cliche" too easily (refer to spoiler above). I couldn't help feel a pang of disappointment. But, in the end, he was just...OK (hence, my 2 star rating). <br><br>Maybe the series just lost its steam, because I had to wait SO long for its release? Then again, maybe it's just me. I realized, my taste in books are shifting. There just has to be some SUBSTANCE though, backing up all the "passionate" sex. Otherwise, it just grosses me out. Blegh. <br><br>One thing is for sure: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16055475.The_Forever_of_Ella_and_Micha__The_Secret___2_" title="The Forever of Ella and Micha (The Secret, #2) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Forever of Ella and Micha</a> might have put me in a perpetual NA funk. *please don't let this be the case* </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_446993533" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/446993533" />
    <a title="Katie(babs)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs"><img alt="Katie(babs)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1242522005p2/179852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/446993533?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie(babs)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie(babs)" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs">Katie(babs)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/179852-katie-babs?shelf=i-want-to-have-babies-with-the-book">i-want-to-have-babies-with-the-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer446993533" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11531385051274240963"> If you were a fan of The Secret of Ella and Micha, you’ll find yourself in love with the sequel, The Forever of Ella and Micha. There’s a powerhouse of emotion on every page with these two incredible characters that Jessica Sorensen has created with Ella and Micha. When the reading community at large talks about the best books in New Adult, right away these two books come to mind. Jessica has a great knack for writing very dimensional and “real” characters and situations. <br/><br/>The Forever of Ella an</span>
  <span id="freeText11531385051274240963" style="display:none"> If you were a fan of The Secret of Ella and Micha, you’ll find yourself in love with the sequel, The Forever of Ella and Micha. There’s a powerhouse of emotion on every page with these two incredible characters that Jessica Sorensen has created with Ella and Micha. When the reading community at large talks about the best books in New Adult, right away these two books come to mind. Jessica has a great knack for writing very dimensional and “real” characters and situations. <br /><br />The Forever of Ella and Micha is written in the same vein as The Secret and Ella and Micha. These two have come very far since the events in the first book, but unfortunately for Ella, she still has deep issues and isn’t sure she can be everything Micha wants her to be. Ella is smart though, and is in therapy and wants to work out her issues and stemming from her mother’s suicide, her alcoholic father and her cold and distant older brother who's getting married. Micha is there for Ella through it all, although he's touring with his band. He has a good shot of hitting it big on the music scene. But he worries about Ella and their future, including his own issues with his father who walked out on Micha and his mother and ended up marrying and creating a new family.<br /><br />Ella is everything to Micha but she still keeps him at arm’s length in some cases, thinking it’s best if they cool things down. Micha isn’t open to that and tries his best to show Ella he can help her heal. There are also some outside sources that may corrode Ella and Micha’s relationship such as jealously, manly from Micha regarding some male attention Ella receives at college and the fact that both have different lifestyles that could put up more walls between them. Micha refuses to give up on Ella and what they have, because Ella is Micha's forever. He just has to prove to Ella that it’s better for them to be together than apart.<br /><br />The Forever of Ella and Micha is like a warm blanket you want to wrap yourself in. Micha really shines here and there are so many aww worthy moments from him. When Ella decides to slow things down, Micha may not be happy but he respects her wishes and does something so lovely such as simply snuggling in bed with Ella and singing to her. Ella tries to remain strong, not only for herself, but for Micha. She doesn’t want to use him as a crutch to get better emotionally. Micha wants Ella to use him in every way from a shoulder to cry on, as a friend and also as a lover.<br /><br />The Forever of Ella and Micha is one of the best books I’ve read this year. Micha and Ella are each other's yin and yang. They are perfect harmony together. The love scenes her are much hotter than the first book, but they fit and aren't thrown in just to titillate. Micha's reactions to Ella when he wants to be intimate is exactly how a guy his age acts. Ella can barely deny Micha, and he knows it, but he never pushes or lays on the guilt.<br /><br />The emo angst isn't over the top and the overall trust and friendship and love is so strong here. I really can’t find any negatives about his book. I’m happy to say this is one of the few books I read this year where I want to have babies with it. You know a book is a true winner when I invoke that phrase. The Forever of Ella and Micha is indeed that and more.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11531385051274240963" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1397280730747217120">When I found out I was approved by Netgalley for this book I think I literally squealed, because it had been a long and torturous wait for more of the beautiful characters I fell in love with in the first book of this series! I adore both Ella and Micha, and I was so anxious to see them find the forever happiness that they had more than earned. Jessica Sorensen has wowed me yet again with this perfect conclusion to their story, and I enjoyed every moment!! Even when she was ripping my heart out </span>
  <span id="freeText1397280730747217120" style="display:none">When I found out I was approved by Netgalley for this book I think I literally squealed, because it had been a long and torturous wait for more of the beautiful characters I fell in love with in the first book of this series! I adore both Ella and Micha, and I was so anxious to see them find the forever happiness that they had more than earned. Jessica Sorensen has wowed me yet again with this perfect conclusion to their story, and I enjoyed every moment!! Even when she was ripping my heart out with the painful roadblocks that Ella and Micha had to make it through, it was all well worth it. Ella was growing up and learning that life was not always going to be perfect, and that it was okay to let Micha see her flaws and have him love her just the same. And Micha was absolutely amazing as the rock that she could turn to, the man that loved her from the depths of his soul even when she was pushing him away. I love this boy!!! Thank you Netgalley for putting me out of my misery by cutting my wait short, and thank you Jessica for giving us such incredible characters to curl up and fall in love with!! <br /><br /><b>~Love you more than life itself, more than the sun and the air. You own my soul, Ella May. ~Micha, Loc 2295 </b><br /><br /><b>"But Ella, we can wait around, wasting years, hoping we'll reach perfection in our lives. But it doesn't exist. We'll always have problems, but as long as we work through them <i>together</i>, I think we'll be okay." ~Micha, Loc2976 </b><br /> </span>

<div id="review_592277212" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/592277212" />
    <a title="Cocktails and Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3769521-cocktails-and-books"><img alt="Cocktails and Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1436217947p2/3769521.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/592277212?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cocktails and Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cocktails and Books" href="/user/show/3769521-cocktails-and-books">Cocktails and Books</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17560336-the-forever-of-ella-and-micha">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3769521-cocktails-and-books?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3769521-cocktails-and-books?shelf=2013-reading-challenge">2013-reading-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer592277212" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7762487845217558560">I wasn't sure what to expect with this book, since I felt like Ella and Micha's story came to a good conclusion in the first book. But Jessica Sorensen gave us an insight into their relationship and solidified what I already knew about the two of them...they were meant to be together.<br/><br/>At the end of The Secret of Ella and Micha, Ella was back in Las Vegas at school and Micha was out touring with the band. They were trying to make the long distance "thing" work while they both worked through issues</span>
  <span id="freeText7762487845217558560" style="display:none">I wasn't sure what to expect with this book, since I felt like Ella and Micha's story came to a good conclusion in the first book. But Jessica Sorensen gave us an insight into their relationship and solidified what I already knew about the two of them...they were meant to be together.<br /><br />At the end of The Secret of Ella and Micha, Ella was back in Las Vegas at school and Micha was out touring with the band. They were trying to make the long distance "thing" work while they both worked through issues with their respective fathers. But the stress of dealing with the issues by themselves took their toll on not only each of them, but their relationship.<br /><br />I have to give a lot of credit to both characters. Ella knew she had issues and was already seeing a therapist. But when she hit bottom, she knew it was important to work on trying to get herself back together and not push forward with a sexual relationship with Micha, not matter how much she wanted it. She was trying to make sure that she didn't go down the same path as her mother and drag those she loved down with her. But the big difference between Ella and her mother was Micha.<br /><br />Micha knew he was meant for Ella and no matter what demons she needed to face he was always going to be there for her. He would give Ella the space she needed, even if it killed him and he always made sure she knew that not matter what she could count on him. Ella's issues tended to overshadow what was happening with Micha, but when he needed her she was there for him.<br /><br />Most of Micha and Ella's issues came from a lack of communication. They both held in what they were feeling when it came to what hurt them most. Once they finally started talking, really talking, with each other, their relationship was able to get onto more solid footing and left me feeling like they were really going to make it.<br /><br />I look forward to Lila and Ethan's story. The foursome need each other and it's very clear these two are meant for each other as well.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7762487845217558560" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer433538781" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6403962502320483242">I was so excited to read this book that I actually put my current book aside to start this the day it was released. I have to say I was slightly disappointed in the book. I can't really pin point the exact reason why, it just wasn't what I thought it would be like. Ella really kind of drove me crazy in this book. I understand she had some serious mental issues but she was inside her head way to much in this book. I was glad she was seeing someone (therapist) for help...in the long run I think it</span>
  <span id="freeText6403962502320483242" style="display:none">I was so excited to read this book that I actually put my current book aside to start this the day it was released. I have to say I was slightly disappointed in the book. I can't really pin point the exact reason why, it just wasn't what I thought it would be like. Ella really kind of drove me crazy in this book. I understand she had some serious mental issues but she was inside her head way to much in this book. I was glad she was seeing someone (therapist) for help...in the long run I think it really helped her. I did think that this book had a little too much drama between Micha and Ella. I guess I didn't see their relationship going the way that the author took them in this book. I will say I was going to give this a 3 star rating but Micha and the ending (epilogue) really saved the book for me. Micha was just as swoon worthy as he was in book 1. <br /><br />I would recommend this book to anyone who has read The Secret of Ella and Micha....this book really finishes their story. I am also looking forward to book 3 The Temptation of Lila and Ethan. I really liked both of those characters in this book. They were such phenomenal friends to both Ella and Micha.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6403962502320483242" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3683762701003798283">Not exactly the "forever" I had imagined in my head for Ella and Micha. Still loving both the characters and wanted so much for this sequel to grab me as powerfully as did the first book. However, I felt a great deal of letdown when the story line was so weak and flimsy.   <span id="freeText3683762701003798283" style="display:none">Not exactly the "forever" I had imagined in my head for Ella and Micha. Still loving both the characters and wanted so much for this sequel to grab me as powerfully as did the first book. However, I felt a great deal of letdown when the story line was so weak and flimsy. It just didn't live up to the emotional ramp I felt they deserved. Yes, Ella and Micha agree on a forever and most likely get that happily ever after but I wanted to see it, feel it, and know it without a doubt. Too rushed and unfinished. This one disappointed.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('daGD8/BlMrG4sd3AsKiEqP8nXj5sCnwFcruBxtK/KZ6nRn/pktz5XgWBRZn6rOr2zb2BLyBptSqA4IClEPbZlw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nNYpJHCilf+iJqE8ZU18e1n+oqkZV12PXal6MlZoRT5OMdU+EhteEB8WOWUvSRIla2R9uFU0lKCv8ntRlCG1Nw==')})
  }
